13 object Utils {
14   import com.github.nscala_time.time.Imports._
15   def toTry[A](either : Either[io.circe.Error, A]) : Try[A] =
16     either match {
17       case Right(categories) => Success(categories)
18       case Left(error) => Failure(new RuntimeException (error.getMessage()))
19       case Json.Null => Failure(new RuntimeException ("Http request is Null"))
20     }
21   def parseTime(str: String): Tuple2[Int, Int] = {
22     val time = DateTimeFormat.forPattern("HH:mm").parseDateTime(str)
23     (time.getHourOfDay, time.getMinuteOfHour)
24   }
25   def bind[A, B](value: Try[A], f: A => B): Try[B] = {
26     value match {
27       case Success(v) => Success(f(v))
28       case Failure(e) => Failure(e)
29     }
30   }
31 }

38   val filename = "config.txt"
39   def writeFile(s: String, filename: String = filename): Unit = {
40     import java.io._
41     val file = new File(filename)
42     val bw = new BufferedWriter(new FileWriter(file))
43     bw.write(s)
44     bw.close()
45   }

47   case class ConfigData(
48       city:     String,
49       categories: List[String],
50       mon:      List[List[String]],
51       tue:      List[List[String]],
52       wed:      List[List[String]],
53       thu:      List[List[String]],
54       fri:      List[List[String]],
55       sat:      List[List[String]],
56       sun:      List[List[String]],
57       days:     Int)
58 
59   def showConfigData(configData: ConfigData): String = {
60     val city = configData.city
61     val cat = configData.categories
62     val mon = configData.mon
63     val tue = configData.tue
64     val wed = configData.wed
65     val thu = configData.thu
66     val fri = configData.fri
67     val sat = configData.sat
68     val sun = configData.sun
69     val days = configData.days
70     val outputList = List(
71       "\n City       = " ++ city.toString,
72       "\n Categories = " ++ (cat mkString ", "),
73       "\n Monday     = " ++ (mon.map(_ mkString " - ") mkString "; " ),
74       "\n Tuesday    = " ++ (tue.map(_ mkString " - ") mkString "; " ),
75       "\n Wednesday  = " ++ (wed.map(_ mkString " - ") mkString "; " ),
76       "\n Thursday   = " ++ (thu.map(_ mkString " - ") mkString "; " ),
77       "\n Friday     = " ++ (fri.map(_ mkString " - ") mkString "; " ),
78       "\n Saturday   = " ++ (sat.map(_ mkString " - ") mkString "; " ),
79       "\n Sunday     = " ++ (sun.map(_ mkString " - ") mkString "; " ),
80       "\n Days       = " ++ days.toString)
81     outputList mkString ""
82   }

84   case class ConfigInternal (
85     city: String,
86     categories: List[String],
87     dates: List[Tuple2[DateTime, DateTime]]
88   )
89 
90     def config(): Try[ConfigData] = {
91         val config = fromFile(filename) mkString ""
92         implicit val decoder: Decoder[ConfigData] = deriveDecoder
93         decode[ConfigData](config) |> toTry
94 
95     }
96     def getDayTimetable(week_num: Int, config: ConfigData): List[List[String]] = {
97         week_num match {
98           case 1 => config.mon
99           case 2 => config.tue
100           case 3 => config.wed
101           case 4 => config.thu
102           case 5 => config.fri
103           case 6 => config.sat
104           case 7 => config.sun
105         }
106     }
107     def updateTime(time: List[String], dateTime: DateTime): Tuple2[DateTime, DateTime] = {
108         time match {
109             case start :: end :: Nil => {
110                 val (h1, m1) = parseTime(start)
111                 val (h2, m2) = parseTime(end)
112                 val dateTime1 = dateTime.hour(h1).minute(m1).withZone(DateTimeZone.UTC)
113                 val dateTime2 = dateTime.hour(h2).minute(m2).withZone(DateTimeZone.UTC)
114                 (dateTime1, dateTime2)
115             }
116         }
117     }
118     def timeConvert(config: ConfigData): List[Tuple2[DateTime, DateTime]] = {
119         var startDate = DateTime.now().second(0)
120         val periods =
121             for (i <- 1 to config.days) yield {
122                 val dayOfWeek: Int = startDate.getDayOfWeek
123                 val lstPeriods = getDayTimetable(dayOfWeek, config)
124                 val list = lstPeriods.map(updateTime(_, startDate))
125                 startDate = startDate.plusDays(1)
126                 list
127             }
128         List(periods).flatten.flatten
129     }
130   def configDataToInternal(configData: ConfigData): ConfigInternal = {
131     val city = configData.city
132     val categories = configData.categories
133     val dates = timeConvert(configData)
134     ConfigInternal(city, categories, dates)
135   }
136   def interactiveSet(configData : ConfigData, field: String, value: String) : Tuple2[ConfigData, String] = {
137     import API._
138     val api = API
139     field match {
140       case "city" => {
141         val cities = api.cities match {
142           case Success(v) => v.map(_.slug)
143           case Failure(e) => return (configData, "Error when trying access city from API")
144         }
145         if (cities.contains(value)) {
146           return (configData.copy(city = value), "")
147         } else {
148           return (configData, value ++ " is not in the list of cities")
149         }
150       }
151       case "days" => {
152         Try(value.toInt) match {
153           case Success(v) => {
154             if (v > 0) {
155               return (configData.copy(days = v), "")
156             } else {
157               return (configData, "Error, days is lower than 0 or equal 0")
158             }
159           }
160         }
161       }
162       case "categories" => {
163         val cat = decode[List[String]](value) |> toTry
164 
165         cat match {
166           case Failure(e) => return (configData, "Error when trying to decode categories")
167           case Success(catV) => {
168             val categories = api.categories match {
169               case Success(v) => v.map(_.slug)
170               case Failure(e) => return (configData, "Error when trying access categories from API")
171             }
172             if (catV.forall(categories.contains(_))) {
173               return (configData.copy(categories = catV), "")
174             } else {
175               return (configData, catV.toString ++ " is not in the list of categories")
176             }
177           }
178         }
179       }
180       case "mon" => {
181         val time = decode[List[List[String]]](value) |> toTry
182         time match {
183           case Success(v) => return (configData.copy(mon = v), "")
184           case Failure(e) => return (configData, "Error when trying to decode time")
185         }
186       }
187       case "tue" => {
188         val time = decode[List[List[String]]](value) |> toTry
189         time match {
190           case Success(v) => return (configData.copy(tue = v), "")
191           case Failure(e) => return (configData, "Error when trying to decode time")
192         }
193       }
194       case "wed" => {
195         val time = decode[List[List[String]]](value) |> toTry
196         time match {
197           case Success(v) => return (configData.copy(wed = v), "")
198           case Failure(e) => return (configData, "Error when trying to decode time")
199         }
200       }
201       case "thu" => {
202         val time = decode[List[List[String]]](value) |> toTry
203         time match {
204           case Success(v) => return (configData.copy(thu = v), "")
205           case Failure(e) => return (configData, "Error when trying to decode time")
206         }
207       }
208       case "fri" => {
209         val time = decode[List[List[String]]](value) |> toTry
210         time match {
211           case Success(v) => return (configData.copy(fri = v), "")
212           case Failure(e) => return (configData, "Error when trying to decode time")
213         }
214       }
215       case "sat" => {
216         val time = decode[List[List[String]]](value) |> toTry
217         time match {
218           case Success(v) => return (configData.copy(sat = v), "")
219           case Failure(e) => return (configData, "Error when trying to decode time")
220         }
221       }
222       case "sun" => {
223         val time = decode[List[List[String]]](value) |> toTry
224         time match {
225           case Success(v) => return (configData.copy(sun = v), "")
226           case Failure(e) => return (configData, "Error when trying to decode time")
227         }
228       }
229 
230     return (configData, "")
231     }
232 
233   }

236 object Interface {

239   val api = API
240   def printTryList[A](list : List[A]) : Try[List[A]] = {
241     println()
242     for(elem <- list) {
243       println(elem)
244     }
245     Try(list)
246   }
247   def printTryCities(list : List[City]) : Try[List[City]] = {
248     println()
249     for(city <- list) {
250       val slug = city.slug
251       val name = city.name
252       println(s"\t- $name - $slug ")
253     }
254     Try(list)
255   }
256 
257   def printTryCategories(list : List[Category]) : Try[List[Category]] = {
258     println()
259     for(cat <- list) {
260       val slug = cat.slug
261       val name = cat.name
262       println(s"\t- $name - $slug ")
263     }
264     Try(list)
265   }
266   def printTry[A](elem : A) : Try[A] = {
267     println()
268     println(elem)
269     Try(elem)
270   }

272   import io.circe.syntax._
273   import Config._
274   val cnf = Config
275 
276   def startPrompt(): Unit = {
277     var configData = ConfigData("",List(),List(),List(),List(),List(),List(),List(),List(),1)
278     while(true) {
279       val cmd = scala.io.StdIn.readLine(">> ")
280       if (cmd == ":q") {
281         return ()
282       }
283       val arrayArgs = cmd.split(" ")
284 
285       val args = if (arrayArgs.length > 1) {
286         Array(arrayArgs(0), arrayArgs(1), arrayArgs.slice(2, arrayArgs.length).mkString(""))
287       } else {
288         arrayArgs
289       }
290       args(0) match {
291         case ":q"           => return ()
292         case "find"         => println(events(configDataToInternal(configData)))
293         case "printConfig"  => println(showConfigData(configData))
294         case "exportConfig" => cnf.writeFile(configData.asJson.toString)
295         case "importConfig" => {
296           cnf.config match {
297             case Success(v) => {configData = v; println(showConfigData(configData))}
298             case Failure(e) => println("Error when trying to read config file")
299           }
300         }
301         case "categories"  => api.categories.flatMap(printTryCategories)
302         case "cities"      => api.cities.flatMap(printTryCities)
303         case "set"         => {
304           val res = cnf.interactiveSet(configData, args(1), args(2))
305           configData = res._1
306           if (res._2 == "") {
307             println(showConfigData(configData))
308           } else {
309             println(res._2)
310           }
311 
312         }
313         case "help"       => {
314           println("find                - try to find events with configurated before parameters in config")
315           println("printConfig         - print current state of configuration")
316           println("importConfig        - load config from config.txt file")
317           println("exportConfig        - save config to config.txt file")
318           println("categories          - to get list of categories")
319           println("cities              - to get list of cities")
320           println("set <field> <value> - set value for config\n  Examples:\n    set mon [[\"12:00\", \"14:00\"]]\n    set city msk\n    set categories [\"theater\"]\n    set days 5")
321           println("help                - to get this message")
322           println(":q                  - to exit")
323         }
324         case _            => println("Unknown command")
325       }
326     }
327 
328   }
329 }

331 object API {
332   import Utils._
333   import Config._
334   import com.github.nscala_time.time.Imports._
335   case class Category(id: Int, slug: String, name: String)
336   type Categories = List[Category]
337   def categories() : Try[Categories] = {
338       val jsonCategories =
339           Http("https://kudago.com/public-api/v1.4/event-categories/")
340             .param("order_by", "id")
341             .asString
342       val str : String = jsonCategories.body
343       decode[Categories](str) |> toTry
344   }
345 
346   case class City(slug: String, name: String)
347   type Cities = List[City]
348 
349   def cities() : Try[Cities] = {
350     val jsonCategories =
351       Http("https://kudago.com/public-api/v1.4/locations/?lang=ru")
352         .asString
353     val str : String = jsonCategories.body
354     implicit val decoder: Decoder[City] = deriveDecoder
355     decode[Cities](str) |> toTry
356   }
357 
358   case class Event(id: Int, title: String, slug: String)
359   case class EventsInternal(count: Int, next: Option[String], previous: Option[String], results: List[Event])
360   def events(config: ConfigInternal): String = {
361     val city = config.city
362     val categories = config.categories
363     val dates = config.dates
364     val events =
365       for((start, end) <- dates)
366       yield {
367         val str = Http("https://kudago.com/public-api/v1.4/events/")
368           .param("page_size", "100")
369           .param("location", city)
370           .param("actual_since", start.toString)
371           .param("actual_until", end.toString)
372           .param("categories", categories mkString ",")
373           .asString
374           .body
375         var eventsInternal = decode[EventsInternal](str) |> toTry
376         if (eventsInternal.isSuccess) {
377           var result = List(eventsInternal.get.results)
378           while(eventsInternal.get.next != None) {
379             eventsInternal = decode[EventsInternal](Http(eventsInternal.get.next.get).asString.body) |> toTry
380             if (eventsInternal.isSuccess) {
381               result = eventsInternal.get.results :: result
382             }
383             else {
384               return eventsInternal match {
385                 case Failure(e) => e.toString
386               }
387             }
388           }
389           result.flatten
390         }
391         else {
392           eventsInternal match {
393             case Failure(e) => e.toString
394           }
395         }
396       }
397 
398     val output =
399       for(((start, end), eventsList: List[Event]) <- dates.zip(events)) yield {
400         val startL = start.withZone(DateTimeZone.forOffsetHours(3))
401         val endL = end.withZone(DateTimeZone.forOffsetHours(3))
402         val startS = startL.toString("EEE HH:mm dd-MM-YYYY")
403         val endS = endL.toString("EEE HH:mm dd-MM-YYYY")
404         val startEnd = s"\n\nStart: $startS; End: $endS; \n\t - "
405         val eventsNames = eventsList.map(x => {val id = x.id; val title = x.title; s"$id - $title"}) mkString "\n\t - "
406         startEnd ++ eventsNames
407       }
408     output mkString ""
409   }
410 
411 }
